                <h3 class="headline"><a href="http://shine.yahoo.com/the-thread-how-to/best-summer-shoes-under--30-151132682.html" class="highlight">Summer Shoes</a> We Want Now</h3>

             <div id="watch-description" class="yt-uix-expander yt-uix-expander-collapsed yt-uix-button-panel"> 
              <div id="watch-description-content"> 
               <div id="watch-description-clip"> 
                <p id="watch-uploader-info"> <strong>Published on <span id="eow-date" class="watch-video-date">Feb 17, 2014</span> </strong> </p> 
                <div id="watch-description-text"> 
                 <p id="eow-description">Novel brain-training research by neuropsychologist Aaron Seitz significantly improved the vision of individual baseball players and may have added up to four or five games to the win column in UCR's 2013 season.</p> 
                </div>

var currentSite=window.location;
var cookieName = "currentExpenderSubject";

function setCookie(cookie_name,lastItem){
   var exp=new Date();
   exp.setDate(exp.getDate()+1);
   document.cookie=" "+cookie_name + "=" +escape(lastItem)+((exp==null) ? "" : ";expires="+exp.toUTCString());
}

function randomNumberX(){
   var randomnumber=Math.floor(Math.random()*11);
   return randomnumber;
}

function del_cookie(name) {
   document.cookie = name + '=; expires=Thu, 01-Jan-70 00:00:01 GMT;';
}
 
function getCookie(cookie_name){
   var allMyCookies =  document.cookie;
   var cookiearray  = allMyCookies.split(';');
   // Now take key value pair out of this array
   for(var i=0; i<cookiearray.length; i++){
      name = cookiearray[i].split('=')[0];
      value = cookiearray[i].split('=')[1];       
      if((''+name+'' == ' '+cookieName+'') || (''+name+'' == ''+cookieName+'')){      
       //alert("Key is : [" + name+ "] and Value is : " + value+(''+name+'' == ' '+cookieName+'')); 
       return (value);
      }
   }
   return "";
}

//Onload Function
document.observe('dom:loaded', function() {
   //Cookies
   var lastExp = getCookie(currentSite);
  //alert(lastExp); 
  if( lastExp != undefined && document.getElementById(lastExp)){
     if(document.getElementById(lastExp).nextSibling != undefined){ 
        control = "off";        
        eval(document.getElementById(lastExp).nextSibling.focus());
        eval(document.getElementById(lastExp).nextSibling.onclick());    
      }
   }
   
});

  //set cookie
  setCookie(cookieName,$(item).previous().id);
  var mainContainer = document.getElementById("main");
  var uls = mainContainer.getElementsByTagName("h3");
  var tmp = "";
  for(i=0;i<uls.length;i++){  
  if(uls[i].nextSibling.nextSibling.nextSibling){
    if(uls[i].nextSibling.nextSibling.nextSibling.style.display!='none' && uls[i].nextSibling.className =='xpander-control xpander-on' ){
     new Effect.toggle($($($(uls[i]).next('.xpander')).identify()),'blind');
     uls[i].nextSibling.toggleClassName('xpander-on');
     if(uls[i].id == item.previousSibling.id){
       uls[i].nextSibling.toggleClassName('xpander-on');
     }
    }
   }
  }

  item.toggleClassName('xpander-on');  

}
